	<script>
		var enableInternalScrolling = true && navigator.appName != 'Microsoft Internet Explorer';

		$(document).ready(function ()
		{
			viewportMinWidth = 1200;
			gAutoPriceUpdate = true;
			//homepagemenuToggle("blah");

				GWCORE.Coupon.useBettingPanel = true;

				GWCORE.Coupon.MIN_NORMAL_BETAMT = 0.5;
				GWCORE.Coupon.MIN_NORMAL_BETUNIT = 0.01;
				GWCORE.Coupon.MIN_EXOTIC_BETAMT1 = 0.5;
				GWCORE.Coupon.MIN_EXOTIC_BETAMT2 = 0.5;
				GWCORE.Coupon.MIN_EXOTIC_BETUNIT = 0.01;
				GWCORE.Coupon.showAllBetsAmount = true;
				GWCORE.Coupon.applyAllBetAmountToMultis = true;
				GWCORE.Coupon.showCouponRetain = true;
				GWCORE.Coupon.boostName = 'Top-Up';
				GWCORE.Coupon.inputMode = 'decimal';
				GWCORE.Coupon.userInputDelay = 750;
				GWCORE.Coupon.LoadCouponSession(true);


			if(enableInternalScrolling) //want to enable scroll bars
			{
				GWCORE.InternalScroll.Initialise();
			}
		});

		var homepagemenuOpenEl;
		function homepagemenuToggle(el)
		{
			$(homepagemenuOpenEl).removeClass("selected");

			$(".homepagemenu > dd").toggle(false);

			if(homepagemenuOpenEl !== el)
			{
				$(el).next().toggle();
				$(el).addClass("selected");
				homepagemenuOpenEl = el;
			}
			else
			{
				homepagemenuOpenEl = undefined;
			}
		}
	</script>

		function SortRace(el, tableID, sortingCol)
		{
			console.log("sorting by " + sortingCol);
			GWCORE.setCookie("racingSortCol", (sortingCol + 1), 10, '/'); //need +1 to exclude 0 as not set

			$(tableID).trigger('sorton', [[[sortingCol, 's']]]);
			$(el).parent().children().removeClass('selected');
			$(el).addClass('selected');
		}
